<date>1541193667629<//date><Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
I had a great experience at Vallejo Open MRI Center.  All the folks there were friendly, helpful, and professional. The facility is clean and comfortable.  This visit was my second.  It took two tries for me to get the procedure done due to my claustrophobic reaction the first try.  The technician was very understanding and the second time went through with absolutely  no problems.   Make sure you arrive early. There is a bit of paperwork. They ask very thorough  health questions.... not just insurance information. It made me feel more at ease, that even though I was not in a hospital, I was dealing with medical personnel. I definitely recommend this office.<//review>

I had lost my voice and was unable to call to inform them.  However, what makes me the most mad is that they did not tell her she was paying an outrageous price when she checked in.

I just went to cancel my membership because I think it is ridiculous.  I also just learned now there is a form to fill out or they can't cancel your payment, and they have to approve your cancellation.

*update: I had reached out to them on the same I posted this initially.  I am attaching their response so that others can be informed since they do not tell you this when you book.  They neglected to include in their response me that if I were to transfer my credits to another person to use, it would be a $10 charge.

I asked if they received my cancellation form via email and to confirm I completed it correctly,  I never got a response from them.<//text>< user_name>

I had to return a pair of Colman steel towed working boots to Big5 because a piece of lumber and a hammer fell on them when my son was working on a school project. He had only had them for 1 day and the leather tore. I am glad he was wearing them when the wood and hammer hit the beginning of the steel toe section because they protected his toes from getting smashed. But I didn't like or think that the leather should have ripped at least 1 inch open. So with my son and husband doubting Big5 would do anything, I took them back for an exchange or refund. The man at the counter was very nice and helpful. He said that he had never seen this before and the boots were a damaged product and check the computer to find that they had 1 pair of side 12 Coleman steel towed boot left. The employee at Big5 said that if it happened again or if their were any other problems with the boots to just bring them back for a refund and try a different manufacture of steel towed boots.
